Mysticboards State Correctional Facility

Welcome to Mysticboards State Correctional Facility, a supermax prison where no one escapes... unless you snitch, that is. Now, most of you are hard-ass gangsters who would kill a man for shit like that.

But last night, Haplo was found dead in his cell (thank god). the snitches bashed his skull in or somethin’. Shit just got real.

And they’ll come for each of you next.

you’ve gotta find the snitches and slit their throats so that you can make it out of this place alive.

Prisoners
1. guy night 3
2. eep day 3
3. AJ
4. iron night 1
5. dr. agon night 2
6. mystic
7. that_kid day 2
8. death butt night 3
9. liquidcraig day 4
10. AngryNarwhal night 2
11. enigmatic day 1

Typical TWG rules apply. No outside PMs, no night talking, no death posts allowed (unless it’s really vengeful or hysterical).

Let me know if you don't get an initial PM.

If you can't read the Google Doc, here's a PDF. (http://www.mysticboards.us/PrisonTWG.pdf)
